<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:volmacht.html>volmacht</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:possibly.html>possibly</a> influenced <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:high.html>High</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:macht.html>macht</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Vollmacht</i>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vore</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vor.html>vor</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:fora.html>fora</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:fore.html>fore</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*furai</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*furi</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> functionally merged <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:most.html>most</a> Germanic languages, <a href = vnd.unilang:including.html>including</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a>.
